 if (newWindow)
 window.open(url, '_blank');
 else
 document.location = url;
 }
 function $(id) { return document.getElementById(id); }
 var loadQueue = [];
 function runOnLoad(fn) { loadQueue.push(fn); }
 window.onload = function() {
 for (var i = 0; i < loadQueue.length; i++)
 loadQueue[i]();
 delete loadQueue;
 };

  .linkify {
    display: inline;

  a:hover, .linkify:hover {

  a.button, .button {

  }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Chrome Version       : 99.0.4844.82 (Official Build) (64-bit) (cohort: Stable) 



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version       : 99.0.4844.82 (Official Build) (64-bit) (cohort: Stable) <!----></span>



<br>





Other browsers tested:



<b class="line"><!---->Other browsers tested:<!----></b>



<br>





    Firefox: OK



<span class="line"><!---->    Firefox: OK<!----></span>



<br>





       Edge: FAIL Version 99.0.1150.55 (Official build) (64-bit)



<span class="line"><!---->       Edge: FAIL Version 99.0.1150.55 (Official build) (64-bit)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





What steps will reproduce the problem?



<b class="line"><!---->What steps will reproduce the problem?<!----></b>



<br>





(1)



<b class="line"><!---->(1)<!----></b>





 Load any page with the POC svg file in an img tags src attribute.



<span class="line"><!----> Load any page with the POC svg file in an img tags src attribute.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





What is the expected result?



<b class="line"><!---->What is the expected result?<!----></b>



<br>





Page renders and doesn't crash.



<span class="line"><!---->Page renders and doesn't crash.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





What happens instead?



<b class="line"><!---->What happens instead?<!----></b>



<br>





Blink render engine crashes.



<span class="line"><!---->Blink render engine crashes.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Additional Information



<span class="line"><!---->Additional Information<!----></span>



<br>





A malformed svg being rendered into the browser can cause a null pointer dereference/memory related crash within the blink render engine. After XSLT Transformation and processing, it appears that the extra_data parameter passed within the blink::FrameLoader::CommitNavigation function is modified due to the function containing commit_reason parameter value of CommitReason:kXSLT.



<span class="line"><!---->A malformed svg being rendered into the browser can cause a null pointer dereference/memory related crash within the blink render engine. After XSLT Transformation and processing, it appears that the extra_data parameter passed within the blink::FrameLoader::CommitNavigation function is modified due to the function containing commit_reason parameter value of CommitReason:kXSLT.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/refs/heads/main/third_party/blink/renderer/core/loader/frame_loader.cc#1051



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/refs/heads/main/third_party/blink/renderer/core/loader/frame_loader.cc#1051"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/refs/heads/main/third_party/blink/renderer/core/loader/frame_loader.cc#1051<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





This empty pointer returned then causes a crash within blink::EmptyLocalFrameClient::CreateDocumentLoader when the extra_data unique_ptr is cleaned after the invocation of MakeGarbageCollected. 



<span class="line"><!---->This empty pointer returned then causes a crash within blink::EmptyLocalFrameClient::CreateDocumentLoader when the extra_data unique_ptr is cleaned after the invocation of MakeGarbageCollected. <!----></span>



<br>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/refs/heads/main/third_party/blink/renderer/core/loader/empty_clients.cc#127



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/refs/heads/main/third_party/blink/renderer/core/loader/empty_clients.cc#127"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/refs/heads/main/third_party/blink/renderer/core/loader/empty_clients.cc#127<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





I've observed this working/crashing both Chrome and Edge, and it appears that anything else using the Blink engine may be affected. Any website that accepts SVG files as upload for images and renders them onto the page within an image tag. I.e: <img src="crash.svg"> would result in a remote DoS for that web page on any application utilizing the blink rendering engine.



<span class="line"><!---->I've observed this working/crashing both Chrome and Edge, and it appears that anything else using the Blink engine may be affected. Any website that accepts SVG files as upload for images and renders them onto the page within an image tag. I.e: &lt;img src="crash.svg"&gt; would result in a remote DoS for that web page on any application utilizing the blink rendering engine.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I have attached some GDB screenshots, a full stack trace, and the proof of concept code (.html and .svg files).



<span class="line"><!---->I have attached some GDB screenshots, a full stack trace, and the proof of concept code (.html and .svg files).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Thank you!



<span class="line"><!---->Thank you!<!----></span>



<br>





Ryan Garbars



<span class="line"><!---->Ryan Garbars<!----></span>

So the problem is the EmptyClient creates a DocumentLoader, but the code casts unconditionally to a WebDocumentLoaderImpl. Having EmptyClient create a WebDocumentLoaderImpl fixes the crash but that leads to a DCHECK in the use counter. 



<span class="line"><!---->So the problem is the EmptyClient creates a DocumentLoader, but the code casts unconditionally to a WebDocumentLoaderImpl. Having EmptyClient create a WebDocumentLoaderImpl fixes the crash but that leads to a DCHECK in the use counter. <!----></span>

Letting the loader and SVG folks triage then.

DocumentLoader.  However, FrameLoader::CommitNavigation static_cast

Will a CVE be assigned to this bug? A remote DoS situation could be pretty bad with this. If a malicious user were to the upload the svg file as a profile picture for a website, all pages that load the svg within an image tag would result in the page being un-renderable for anyone using a browser/application with the Blink engine (Chrome, Edge, etc) due this crash caused by the wrong type creation.



<span class="line"><!---->Will a CVE be assigned to this bug? A remote DoS situation could be pretty bad with this. If a malicious user were to the upload the svg file as a profile picture for a website, all pages that load the svg within an image tag would result in the page being un-renderable for anyone using a browser/application with the Blink engine (Chrome, Edge, etc) due this crash caused by the wrong type creation.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->Date: Mon May 02 00:09:48 2022<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Do not update use counter twice for XSLT transformation.



<span class="line"><!---->Do not update use counter twice for XSLT transformation.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





If XSLT is used inside an SVG image, document will be replaced when



<span class="line"><!---->If XSLT is used inside an SVG image, document will be replaced when<!----></span>



<br>





XSLT finishes processing.  In that case, use counter would be called



<span class="line"><!---->XSLT finishes processing.  In that case, use counter would be called<!----></span>



<br>





twice.  To prevent it is called twice, we do not call DidCommitLoad



<span class="line"><!---->twice.  To prevent it is called twice, we do not call DidCommitLoad<!----></span>



<br>





if the document has been replaced.



<span class="line"><!---->if the document has been replaced.<!----></span>



<br>

Switching to type=Bug-security and cc'ing folks so they don't lose access.



<span class="line"><!---->Switching to type=Bug-security and cc'ing folks so they don't lose access.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Thanks for checking whether this should get a CVE. It's not entirely clear, but I think probably so. For that reason I'm reclassifying this as type=Bug-Security which will result in all the right things happening.



<span class="line"><!---->Thanks for checking whether this should get a CVE. It's not entirely clear, but I think probably so. For that reason I'm reclassifying this as type=Bug-Security which will result in all the right things happening.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Labelling up:



<span class="line"><!---->Labelling up:<!----></span>



<br>





FoundIn-99 - assuming the original report is correct



<span class="line"><!---->FoundIn-99 - assuming the original report is correct<!----></span>



<br>





Security_Severity-High - this appears to be type confusion within Blink. Therefore, this could potentially be used to achieve remote code execution inside the renderer process.



<span class="line"><!---->Security_Severity-High - this appears to be type confusion within Blink. Therefore, this could potentially be used to achieve remote code execution inside the renderer process.<!----></span>



<br>





OS - assuming it affects all Blink platforms



<span class="line"><!---->OS - assuming it affects all Blink platforms<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Neither DoS bugs nor null pointer dereferences count as Chrome security bugs (for reasons described in the FAQ here - 



<span class="line"><!---->Neither DoS bugs nor null pointer dereferences count as Chrome security bugs (for reasons described in the FAQ here - <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/master/docs/security/faq.md



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/master/docs/security/faq.md"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/master/docs/security/faq.md<!----></a>





)



<span class="line"><!---->)<!----></span>





 but type confusion or a double deletion is potentially exploitable, so I think we should err on the side of caution here and regard this as a security bug.



<span class="line"><!----> but type confusion or a double deletion is potentially exploitable, so I think we should err on the side of caution here and regard this as a security bug.<!----></span>

Hello Ryan, thank you for this report, however, all evidence via the POC, stack trace, and analysis points to this issue being a null pointer deref and resulting in a denial of service. Neither null ptr derefs [1] and denial of service [2] are considered security bugs in Chrome's threat model; therefore, this issue does not appear to be a security bug and is not eligible for a VRP reward. 



<span class="line"><!---->Hello Ryan, thank you for this report, however, all evidence via the POC, stack trace, and analysis points to this issue being a null pointer deref and resulting in a denial of service. Neither null ptr derefs [1] and denial of service [2] are considered security bugs in Chrome's threat model; therefore, this issue does not appear to be a security bug and is not eligible for a VRP reward. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





If you are able to demonstrate this type confusion bug is exploitable to result in security implication such as memory corruption to allow for RCE, we would happily reassess for a potential VRP reward. 



<span class="line"><!---->If you are able to demonstrate this type confusion bug is exploitable to result in security implication such as memory corruption to allow for RCE, we would happily reassess for a potential VRP reward. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->[1] <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src/+/refs/heads/main/docs/security/faq.md#Why-aren_t-null-pointer-dereferences-considered-security-bugs

        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;

          z-index: 999;

          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */

        }

          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }

          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
